<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


### PREPARAÇÃO DE DADOS PARA CÁLCULO DE LPI

Carregar dados. O arquivo `dadosICMBio_2014a2019.rds` deve ser gerado na etapa anterior através de `part01-fixRawData.Rmd`


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxubXlkYXRhIDwtIHJlYWRSRFMoaGVyZShcIjAzX2RhZG9zRGVTYWlkYS9kYWRvc1wiLCBcImRhZG9zSUNNQmlvXzIwMTRhMjAxOS5yZHNcIikpXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
mydata <- readRDS(here("03_dadosDeSaida/dados", "dadosICMBio_2014a2019.rds"))
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-chunk-end -->


<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


CONTAGENS:
- UCs
- Espécies
- Populações

<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuI0NvbnRhZ2VtIGRlIFVDc1xudWNzIDwtIG15ZGF0YSAlPiVcbiAgZ3JvdXBfYnkoY251Yyxub21lX1VDKSAlPiVcbiAgY291bnQoKVxuI0NvbnRhZ2VtIGRlIGVzcMOpY2llc1xuc3AgPC0gbXlkYXRhICU+JVxuICBncm91cF9ieShjbGFzc2UsIG9yZGVtLCBmYW1pbGlhLCBnZW5lcm8sIGJpbm9taWFsKSAlPiVcbiAgY291bnQoKSAlPiVcbiAgYXJyYW5nZShkZXNjKG4pKVxuI0NvbnRhZ2VtIGRlIHBvcHVsYcOnw7Vlc1xucG9wdWxhdGlvbiA8LSBteWRhdGEgJT4lXG4gIGdyb3VwX2J5KG5vbWVfVUMsIHBvcHVsYWNhbywgY251YykgJT4lXG4gIGNvdW50KCkgJT4lXG4gIGFycmFuZ2UoZGVzYyhuKSkgJT4lXG4gIGZpbHRlcigpXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
#Contagem de UCs
ucs <- mydata %>%
  group_by(cnuc,nome_UC) %>%
  count()
#Contagem de espécies
sp <- mydata %>%
  group_by(classe, ordem, familia, genero, binomial) %>%
  count() %>%
  arrange(desc(n))
#Contagem de populações
population <- mydata %>%
  group_by(nome_UC, populacao, cnuc) %>%
  count() %>%
  arrange(desc(n)) %>%
  filter()
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-chunk-end -->


<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


Cálculo de esforço


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuZWZmb3J0IDwtIG15ZGF0YSAlPiVcbiNBR1JVUEFSIFBPREUgVU5JREFERSBERSBDT05TRVJWQcOHw4NPIEUgQU5PXG4gIGdyb3VwX2J5KGNudWMsIG5vbWVfVUMsIGFubykgJT4lXG4jU09NQVIgRVNGT1LDh08gQU5VQUwgUE9SIFVOSURBREUgREUgQ09OU0VSVkHDh8ODT1xuICBzdW1tYXJpemUoc3VtKGVzZm9yY28sIG5hLnJtID0gVFJVRSkpICU+JVxuI1JFTk9NRUFSIENPTFVOQSBSRVNVTFRBTlRFXG4gIHJlbmFtZShlZmZvcnQgPSBcInN1bShlc2ZvcmNvLCBuYS5ybSA9IFRSVUUpXCIpICMlPiVcbmBgYCJ9 -->

```r
effort <- mydata %>%
#AGRUPAR PODE UNIDADE DE CONSERVAÇÃO E ANO
  group_by(cnuc, nome_UC, ano) %>%
#SOMAR ESFORÇO ANUAL POR UNIDADE DE CONSERVAÇÃO
  summarize(sum(esforco, na.rm = TRUE)) %>%
#RENOMEAR COLUNA RESULTANTE
  rename(effort = "sum(esforco, na.rm = TRUE)") #%>%
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-output-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYHN1bW1hcmlzZSgpYCBoYXMgZ3JvdXBlZCBvdXRwdXQgYnkgJ2NudWMnLCAnbm9tZV9VQycuIFlvdSBjYW4gb3ZlcnJpZGVcbnVzaW5nIHRoZSBgLmdyb3Vwc2AgYXJndW1lbnQuXG4ifQ== -->

```
`summarise()` has grouped output by 'cnuc', 'nome_UC'. You can override
using the `.groups` argument.
```



<!-- rnb-output-end -->

<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuI0ZJTFRSQVIgUEVMTyBRVUUgU0VSSUEgTyBFU0ZPUsOHTyBNw41OSU1PXG4gICNmaWx0ZXIoZWZmb3J0ID4gMTQ5KVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
#FILTRAR PELO QUE SERIA O ESFORÇO MÍNIMO
  #filter(effort > 149)
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-chunk-end -->


<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


### Seleção por critérios

Selecionar UCs Seleção de UCs com mais de 1 ano de amostragem e mais de 149 km de esforço anual.


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxudWNzX3NlbGVjaW9uYWRhcyA8LSBlZmZvcnQgJT4lXG4gIGdyb3VwX2J5KGNudWMpICU+JSBcbiAgY291bnQoKSAlPiVcbiAgZmlsdGVyKG4gPiAxKSAlPiVcbiAgcHVsbChjbnVjKVxudWNzX3NlbGVjaW9uYWRhc1xuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
ucs_selecionadas <- effort %>%
  group_by(cnuc) %>% 
  count() %>%
  filter(n > 1) %>%
  pull(cnuc)
ucs_selecionadas
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-output-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiIFsxXSAgIDQ3ICAgNjAgICA3NiAgMTE4ICAxMzYgIDE0MiAgMTQzICAxNDggIDE0OSAgMTUxICAxNTIgIDE2OSAgMTcyXG5bMTRdICAxNzMgIDE4NyAgMTg4ICAxODkgIDIwNyAgMjA4ICAyMTEgIDIxMyAgMjIxICAyMjIgIDIzMiAgMjU2ICAyNThcblsyN10gIDI1OSAgMjc0ICAyODEgMTYzMyAxODEwXG4ifQ== -->

```
 [1]   47   60   76  118  136  142  143  148  149  151  152  169  172
[14]  173  187  188  189  207  208  211  213  221  222  232  256  258
[27]  259  274  281 1633 1810
```

<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


Filtrar

Filtrar dados gerais mantendo somente UCs selecionadas


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxubXlkYXRhIDwtIG15ZGF0YSAlPiVcbiAgZmlsdGVyKGNudWMgJWluJSB1Y3Nfc2VsZWNpb25hZGFzKVxubXlkYXRhXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
mydata <- mydata %>%
  filter(cnuc %in% ucs_selecionadas)
mydata
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


Esforço anual em km


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuZXNmb3Jjb19hbnVhbCA8LSBteWRhdGEgJT4lXG4gIGdyb3VwX2J5KGNudWMsIGFubykgJT4lXG4gIHN1bW1hcml6ZShlc2ZvcmNvID0gc3VtKGVzZm9yY28sIG5hLnJtID0gVFJVRSkpXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
esforco_anual <- mydata %>%
  group_by(cnuc, ano) %>%
  summarize(esforco = sum(esforco, na.rm = TRUE))
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-output-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYHN1bW1hcmlzZSgpYCBoYXMgZ3JvdXBlZCBvdXRwdXQgYnkgJ2NudWMnLiBZb3UgY2FuIG92ZXJyaWRlIHVzaW5nIHRoZVxuYC5ncm91cHNgIGFyZ3VtZW50LlxuIn0= -->

```
`summarise()` has grouped output by 'cnuc'. You can override using the
`.groups` argument.
```



<!-- rnb-output-end -->

<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuZXNmb3Jjb0FudWFsUmVwb3J0IDwtIG15ZGF0YSAlPiVcbiAgZ3JvdXBfYnkoY251Yyxub21lX1VDLCBhbm8pICU+JVxuICBzdW1tYXJpemUoZXNmb3JjbyA9IHN1bShlc2ZvcmNvLCBuYS5ybSA9IFRSVUUpKVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
esforcoAnualReport <- mydata %>%
  group_by(cnuc,nome_UC, ano) %>%
  summarize(esforco = sum(esforco, na.rm = TRUE))
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-output-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYHN1bW1hcmlzZSgpYCBoYXMgZ3JvdXBlZCBvdXRwdXQgYnkgJ2NudWMnLCAnbm9tZV9VQycuIFlvdSBjYW4gb3ZlcnJpZGVcbnVzaW5nIHRoZSBgLmdyb3Vwc2AgYXJndW1lbnQuXG4ifQ== -->

```
`summarise()` has grouped output by 'cnuc', 'nome_UC'. You can override
using the `.groups` argument.
```

<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->

```r
esforco_anual_wide <- esforco_anual %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = ano, values_from = esforco) %>%
  select(cnuc,
         `2014`,
         `2015`,
         `2016`,
         `2017`,
         `2018`,
         `2019`
         ) %>%
  ungroup()

esforcoAnualWideReport <- esforcoAnualReport %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = ano, values_from = esforco) %>%
  select(cnuc,
         nome_UC,
         `2014`,
         `2015`,
         `2016`,
         `2017`,
         `2018`,
         `2019`
         ) %>%
  ungroup()

```

Número de registros anuais


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuI07Dmk1FUk8gREUgUkVHSVNUUk9TIEFOw4FMSVNFXG5uX3JlZ2lzdHJvcyA8LSBteWRhdGEgJT4lXG4gIGdyb3VwX2J5KGNudWMsIGFubywgcG9wdWxhY2FvKSAlPiVcbiAgY291bnQoKSAjJT4lXG4gIyBtdXRhdGUobiA9IGFzLm51bWVyaWMobikpXG4jTsOaTUVSTyBERSBSRUdJU1RST1MgUEFSQSBPIFJFTEFUw5NSSU9cbm5SZWdpc3Ryb3NSZXBvcnQgPC0gbXlkYXRhICU+JVxuICBncm91cF9ieShjbnVjLCBub21lX1VDLCBhbm8sIHBvcHVsYWNhbykgJT4lXG4gIGNvdW50KCkgIyU+JVxuICMgbXV0YXRlKG4gPSBhcy5udW1lcmljKG4pKVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
#NÚMERO DE REGISTROS ANÁLISE
n_registros <- mydata %>%
  group_by(cnuc, ano, populacao) %>%
  count() #%>%
 # mutate(n = as.numeric(n))
#NÚMERO DE REGISTROS PARA O RELATÓRIO
nRegistrosReport <- mydata %>%
  group_by(cnuc, nome_UC, ano, populacao) %>%
  count() #%>%
 # mutate(n = as.numeric(n))
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

Número de registros anuais em formato *wide*


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxuI1BBUkEgQU7DgUxJU0Vcbm5fcmVnaXN0cm9zX3dpZGUgPC0gbl9yZWdpc3Ryb3MgJT4lXG4gIHBpdm90X3dpZGVyKG5hbWVzX2Zyb20gPSBhbm8sIHZhbHVlc19mcm9tID0gbikgJT4lXG4gIHNlbGVjdChjbnVjLFxuICAgICAgICAgcG9wdWxhY2FvLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMTRgLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMTVgLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMTZgLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMTdgLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMThgLFxuICAgICAgICAgYDIwMTlgXG4gICAgICAgICApICU+JVxuICByZXBsYWNlKGlzLm5hKC4pLCAwKSAlPiVcbiAgdW5ncm91cCgpXG5uX3JlZ2lzdHJvc193aWRlXG5gYGAifQ== -->

```r
#PARA ANÁLISE
n_registros_wide <- n_registros %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = ano, values_from = n) %>%
  select(cnuc,
         populacao,
         `2014`,
         `2015`,
         `2016`,
         `2017`,
         `2018`,
         `2019`
         ) %>%
  replace(is.na(.), 0) %>%
  ungroup()
n_registros_wide
```

```r
#PARA RELATÓRIO
nRegistrosWideReport <- nRegistrosReport %>%
  pivot_wider(names_from = ano, values_from = n) %>%
  select(cnuc,
         nome_UC,
         populacao,
         `2014`,
         `2015`,
         `2016`,
         `2017`,
         `2018`,
         `2019`
         ) %>%
  replace(is.na(.), 0) %>%
  ungroup()
#n_registros_report

```

<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


### Taxa de encontro anual

Estimativa de abundância relativa (número de registros por esforço). Neste caso *NAs* devem ser mantidos.


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxudGF4YXNfYW51YWlzIDwtIGRhdGEuZnJhbWUobl9yZWdpc3Ryb3Nfd2lkZSlcbmVzZm9yY29zX2FudWFpcyA8LSBkYXRhLmZyYW1lKGVzZm9yY29fYW51YWxfd2lkZSlcbmZvcihpIGluIDE6bnJvdyh0YXhhc19hbnVhaXMpKSB7XG4gIGNudWNfdGVtcCA8LSB0YXhhc19hbnVhaXNbaSwgXCJjbnVjXCJdXG4gIGVzZm9yY29fdGVtcCA8LSBlc2ZvcmNvc19hbnVhaXMgJT4lIGZpbHRlcihjbnVjID09IGNudWNfdGVtcCkgJT4lIHNlbGVjdCgtY251YylcbiAgdGF4YXNfYW51YWlzW2ksIDM6OF0gPC0gcm91bmQodGF4YXNfYW51YWlzW2ksIDM6OF0vZXNmb3Jjb190ZW1wLCAzKVxufVxudGF4YXNfYW51YWlzIDwtIGFzX3RpYmJsZSh0YXhhc19hbnVhaXMpXG50YXhhc19hbnVhaXMgJT4lXG4gIHByaW50KG49SW5mKVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
taxas_anuais <- data.frame(n_registros_wide)
esforcos_anuais <- data.frame(esforco_anual_wide)
for(i in 1:nrow(taxas_anuais)) {
  cnuc_temp <- taxas_anuais[i, "cnuc"]
  esforco_temp <- esforcos_anuais %>% filter(cnuc == cnuc_temp) %>% select(-cnuc)
  taxas_anuais[i, 3:8] <- round(taxas_anuais[i, 3:8]/esforco_temp, 3)
}
taxas_anuais <- as_tibble(taxas_anuais)
taxas_anuais %>%
  print(n=Inf)
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

Selecionar populações com taxa de avistamento média acima de 0.1 (1 ind/10km)


<!-- rnb-text-end -->


<!-- rnb-chunk-begin -->


<!-- rnb-source-begin eyJkYXRhIjoiYGBgclxudGF4YXNfYW51YWlzIDwtIHRheGFzX2FudWFpcyAlPiVcbiAgbXV0YXRlKG1lZGlhID0gcm93TWVhbnMoLlssMzo4XSkpICU+JVxuICBmaWx0ZXIobWVkaWEgPiAwLjEpICU+JVxuICBzZWxlY3QoLW1lZGlhKVxuXG5wcmludCh0YXhhc19hbnVhaXMsIG49SW5mKVxuYGBgIn0= -->

```r
taxas_anuais <- taxas_anuais %>%
  mutate(media = rowMeans(.[,3:8])) %>%
  filter(media > 0.1) %>%
  select(-media)

print(taxas_anuais, n=Inf)
```

<!-- rnb-source-end -->

<!-- rnb-text-begin -->


taxas_anuaisLonger <- taxas_anuais[,-1]
taxas_anuais <-
taxas_anuaisLonger %>%
    pivot_longer(!populacao, names_to = "ano", values_to = "index")

taxas_anuais$cnuc <- substring(taxas_anuais$populacao,nchar(taxas_anuais$populacao)-2,nchar(taxas_anuais$populacao))
taxas_anuais <- merge(taxas_anuais,ucs, by =  "cnuc")
taxas_anuais$especie <- substr(taxas_anuais$populacao,1,nchar(taxas_anuais$populacao)-4)
taxas_anuais$especie <- gsub("_"," ", taxas_anuais$especie)
taxas_anuais$ano <- gsub("X","", taxas_anuais$ano)
#taxas_anuaisTeste <- taxas_anuais[,2:8]
